Aether Crystal
Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction

creatures.

Aether Crystal
item when destroyed.

Aether Crystal Cluster
Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction
Aetherials
Aether Crystals Clusters are
Aetherial
creatures.
They possess the same skills as
Aether Crystals
but have additional resistances and spawn 3 levels higher than the player (thus using skills at a higher level).
Abilities
Summon Zombie
Summons 3
Walking Dead
8 Second Cooldown
6 Summon Limit
Aether Tendril
Aether Damage
3% reduction to Current Life
Aether Field (buff)
(4.5 to 10.5) Meter Radius
Aether Damage
5-10% reduction to Current Life
Reflects 8% Damage

Pierce
50
Bleeding
100
Fire
15

30

Aether Crystal Formation
Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction
Aetherials
Aether Crystals Formations are
Aetherial
creatures.
A larger version of the
Aether Crystals
, they possess the same skills but have additional resistances, and spawn 5 levels higher than the player (thus using skills at a higher level).
Abilities
Summon Aetherfire Zombie

5 Summon Limit

Aether Damage
5-10% reduction to Current Life
Reflects 8% Damage

Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction
Aetherials

Aetherial
creatures. They will spawn from certain Aether Crystal Clusters when destroyed.

offensive buff

Aether Damage
Aether Shard Retaliation

Aether Damage
Aether Waves
20 meter Wave Distance
Physical Damage
Aether Damage
-20% Total Speed for 4 Seconds

8 Summon Limit

Aetherial Crawler
Race
Aetherial
Type
Common
Faction
Aetherial Vanguard
Aetherial Crawlers
are a type of
Aetherial
creature, found throughout
Act 6
. They are summoned by Aetherial
Fleshweavers
.

Vitality: 30%

Aetherial Gutburrower
Race
Aetherial
Type
Common
Faction
Aetherial Vanguard
Aetherial Gutburrowers
are a type of
Aetherial
creature, found throughout
Act 6
. They spawn from slain
Aetherial Regurgitators
.
Abilities
Passive
Physical Damage
Aether Damage
8% Chance of +40% Physical Damage
10% Pierce Resistance
Poison Retaliation
Aether Spit
1 Projectile
2.5 Meter Radius
Aether Damage
Resistances
Physical
25%
Pierce
35%
Aether
25%
Sleep
500%
Stun
500%
Knockdown
500%
Trap
500%
Freeze
500%
Petrify
500%

Aetherial Obelisk
Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction
Aetherials
Aetherial Obelisks are
Aetherial
creatures.
The  Obelisk has 2 forms. in the first it is anchored to the ground, in the 2nd (at 50% Health) it breaks free and adds a spinning Ground Slam ability.

Aether Damage

Vitality: 30%

Aetherial Sentinel
Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction
Aetherial Vanguard
Aetherial Sentinels
are a type of
Aetherial
creature, found throughout
Act 6
. On death they spawn a 2nd-stage
Aetherial Terraformer
.
Abilities
Skill Name
Skill Type
Damage Type
Passive
Physical Damage

Aetherial Terraformer
Race
Aetherial
Type
Champion
Faction
Aetherials
Aetherial Terraformers are
Aetherial
creatures. They are a more powerful form of the
Aetherial Obelisk
.
The  Terraformer has 2 forms. in the first it is anchored to the ground, in the 2nd (at 50% Health) it breaks free and gains additional skills:
Claw Spin
and
Aether Slam
.

Faction

Ascended Attendant
Race
Aetherial
Type
Common
Faction
Aetherial Vanguard
Ascended Attendants
are a type of
Aetherial
creature, found throughout
Act 6
. On death they will spawn an
Aetherial Wraith
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Councilman Garl
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Councilman_Garl
======================================================================

Councilman Garl
Race
Aether Corruption
Type
Boss
Faction
Aetherials
Councilman Garl
is a final Boss creature for
Port Valbury
. He spawns together with
Overlord Van Aldritch
and
Councilman Hallos
.
The three pass around Aldritch's Scepter, indicated by an icon above their head. Whichever holds the scepter gains the
Scepter Storm
buff and the
Aetherbolt Nova
skill.
Aditionally, On death, Councilman Garl confers another buff on remaining allies (see below).
Abilities
Scepter Storm
40% Damage Absorption
+40/60% Total Damage
+20/50% Life Reegneration
Scepter Aetherbolt Nova
8 Projectiles in a 360 Degree Radius
Aether Damage
Fire Damage
Burn Damage over 5 Seconds
30% Total Resistance Reduction for 5 seconds
1 second of Stun
Aether Shard
1 Projectile
3 Meter Explosion Radius
5 Second Duration
Aether Damage
Aether Burst
18 Meter Range
Aether Damage
Burn Damage over 5 Seconds
Reduced Defensive Ability for 5 Seconds
Aethershield
Casts on 20% Life
12 Second Duration
90 Second Cooldown
70% Damage Absorption
+60% Total Damage
Aether Zap
Aether Damage
Vitality Damage
35% reduced Total Speed for 2 seconds
Poison Nova
12 Projectiles in a 360 Degree Radius
Physical Damage
Acid Damage
Poison Damage over 2 Seconds
30% Total Resistance Reduction for 5 seconds
1 second of Stun
Poison Fumes
6 Meter Radius
6 Second Duration
Poison Damage
25% Chance to Fumble for 2 Seconds
-15% Resistances for 2 Seconds
Death Buff
50 Meter Radius
600 second Duration
+80% Total Damage
+15% Crit Damage
+35% Cast Speed
+5% Offensive Ability
+4% Defensive Ability
12% Damage Absorption
20% Skill Cooldown Reduction
Resistances
Level 4

Physical: 30%
Pierce: 35%
Lightning: 33%
Knockdown: 500%

======================================================================

CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures

Councilman Hallos
Race
Aether Corruption
Type
Boss
Faction
Aetherials
Councilman Hallos
is a final Boss creature for
Port Valbury
. He spawns together with
Overlord Van Aldritch
and
Councilman Garl
.
The three pass around Aldritch's Scepter, indicated by an icon above their head. Whichever holds the scepter gains the
Scepter Storm
buff and the
Aetherbolt Nova
skill.
Aditionally, On death, Councilman Hallos confers another buff on remaining allies (see below).
Abilities
Scepter Storm
40% Damage Absorption
+40/60% Total Damage
+20/50% Life Reegneration
Scepter Aetherbolt Nova
8 Projectiles in a 360 Degree Radius
Aether Damage
Fire Damage
Burn Damage over 5 Seconds
30% Total Resistance Reduction for 5 seconds
1 second of Stun

1 Projectile
3 Meter Explosion Radius
5 Second Duration
Aether Damage

18 Meter Range
Aether Damage
Burn Damage over 5 Seconds
Reduced Defensive Ability for 5 Seconds

12 Second Duration
90 Second Cooldown
70% Damage Absorption
+60% Total Damage

6 Second Duration

.

======================================================================
PAGE: Fleshweaver Krieg
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Fleshweaver_Krieg
======================================================================

Fleshweaver Krieg
is a unique
Boss
Monster. Is found in the northwest corner of the
Fleshworks
, accessible from the
The Infestation
.
When spawning at level 94 or above, Fleshweaver Krieg can drop the Chestguard and Mask from the
Krieg's Armament
Legendary Set (4% chance for each). He is best farmed in
Elite
difficulty, as the drop chance is the same as in
Ultimate
.

Gazer Prime
is a secret Giant Gazer boss in
The Shattered Realm
in a shard that looks like its from the Fleshworks. He drops the
Void Orb
for the Hungerling
cosmetic pet
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Herald of Destruction
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Herald_of_Destruction
======================================================================

The
Herald of Destruction
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in
The Immolation
. To enter the area the player must have the quest
Legion Retribution
however. He must be killed to complete this quest.
The Boss fight is divided in two phases, The Herald is first anchored to the ground, attacking the player and summoning Overminds.
Once 50% of it's health bar is depleted, the boss releases itself and flies over the battlefield.
Family:
Aetherial
Genus:
Aetherial Obelisk
Stage 1 (Anchored Form)
Abilities
Lightning Strike
Electrical Aura
Vindictive Aether
Summon Overmind
Skyshard Devastation
Lightning Discharge

Level 3

Cold Resistance 15%
Fire Resistance 15%
Lightning Resistance 75%
Stage 2 (Flying Form)
Abilities
Lightning Strike

======================================================================
PAGE: Herald of the Flame
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Herald_of_the_Flame
======================================================================

The
Herald of the Flame
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in
The Conflagration
. It's located near the cannons required for the
Lost Armaments
quest.
The Boss fight is divided into two phases. The Herald is first anchored to the ground, attacking the player and summoning Fleshwarped Mutants.
Once 50% of its health bar is depleted, the boss releases itself and flies over the battlefield. He will then summon
Flesh Hulk
creatures.
Family:
Aetherial
Genus:
Aetherial Obelisk
Stage 1 (Anchored Form)
Abilities
Zap
Aether Strike
Despair Aura
Vindictive Aether
Summon
Fleshwarped Thrasher
Summon
Fleshwarped Butcher
Aether Conflagration
Resistances
Level 3
Hero/Boss Resistances
Cold Resistance 15%
Fire Resistance 75%
Lightning Resistance 15%
Stage 2 (Flying Form)
Abilities
Zap
Aether Strike
Despair Aura
Vindictive Aether
Summon
Flesh Hulk
Flame Wave
Aether Slam
Claw Spin
Aether Conflagration
Resistances
Level 3
Hero/Boss Resistances
Cold Resistance 15%
Fire Resistance 75%
Lightning Resistance 15%
Notable Drops
Supreme Spoils
Tip
As with seemingly all crystal formations, the first Phase can be outranged with a ranged weapon.

======================================================================
PAGE: Noveria Stormfire
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Noveria_Stormfire
======================================================================

Noveria Stormfire
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in
Stonerend Quarry
. Killing her is necessary to obtain the
Aetherial Essence
required to complete the
A Catalyst
quest.
Noveria will be encountered again as a Ghost during the
Service Beyond Death
quest.
Family:
Aetherial
-
Human
Genus:
Possessed
Abilities
Arcane Missile
Arcane Nova
Arcane Shield
Teleport
Aether Trap
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Aether Resistance 30%
Lightning Resistance 30%
Notable Drops
Grand Spoils
Aetherial Essence
(Quest)

======================================================================
PAGE: Overlord Van Aldritch
CATEGORIES: Aetherial, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Overlord_Van_Aldritch
======================================================================

Overlord Van Aldritch
Race
Aether Corruption
Type
Boss
Faction
Aetherials
Overlord Van Aldritch
is the final Boss creature for
Port Valbury
. He spawns together with
Councilman Garl
and
Councilman Hallos
.
The three pass around Aldritch's Scepter, indicated by an icon above their head. Whichever holds the scepter gains the
Scepter Storm
buff and the
Aetherbolt Nova
Skill.
Aditionally, On death, Overlord Van Aldritch confers another buff on remaining Councillors (see below).
Lore
After the fate of Port Valbury was sealed, the Aetherial known as Aldritch shed its human form and embraced the tainted nature of the Aether itself. Having turned the entire council of Valbury under its sway, it now rules over the fallen city with a strange relic known as the Scepter of Aldritch in hand.
Abilities
Scepter Storm
40% Damage Absorption
+40/60% Total Damage
+20/50% Life Regeneration

8 Projectiles in a 360 Degree Radius

+60% Total Damage

======================================================================
PAGE: Terrnox
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Terrnox
======================================================================

Terrnox
is a unique
Boss
Monster. He has three spawn points in the
Burning Cellar
.
When spawning at level 94 or above, Terrnox can drop the Boots of the
Krieg's Armament
Legendary Set (4.8% chance). He is best farmed in
Elite
difficulty, as the drop chance is the same as in
Ultimate
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Valaxteria
CATEGORIES: Aetherials, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Valaxteria
======================================================================

Valaxteria
is a unique
Boss
Monster. She has a single spawn point in
Crown Hill
, in the building to the left of the Corrupted
Shrine
.
When spawning at level 94 or above, Valaxteria can drop the Shoulders and Gloves of the
Krieg's Armament
Legendary Set (3.5% chance for each). She is best farmed in
Elite
difficulty, as the drop chance is the same as in
Ultimate
.
